<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Salvette</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">salvietta</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салфетка.html>салфе́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">salfétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салфетка.html>салфе́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салфетка.html>салфе́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салфетка.html>салфе́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>napkin, serviette</li>
<li>doily</li>
<li>(wet) wipe</li></ol>

***сальный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льный</a> (19155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sálo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)са́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)са́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> animal fat, lard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:железо.html>железа́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sálʹnaja</b> železá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fat gland</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tallow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свечка.html>све́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sálʹnaja</b> svéčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tallow candle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>containing a high percentage of fat <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of an animal breed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>left by fat <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of a spot or mark</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>greasy</li></ol>

***сам.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> (72)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*samъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*SomHós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sam</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>neuter</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>само́</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сама́</a></b>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>са́ми</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">definitive pronoun<span class="ib-comma">,</span> emphatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> self, -self

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:самодеятельность.html>самоде́ятельность</a> (9100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самодеятельный.html>самоде́ятельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samodéjatelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самодеятельность.html>самоде́ятельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">samodéjatelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самодеятельность.html>самоде́ятельности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самодеятельность.html>самоде́ятельности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самодеятельность.html>самоде́ятельностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>amateur performance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клуб</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:самодеятельность.html>самоде́ятельности</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">klub <b>samodéjatelʹnosti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">amateur club (such as singing, dancing, theatre, etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>initiative, spontaneous action</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">само-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наде́ять(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadéjatʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-янный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самонадеянный.html>самонаде́янный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">samonadéjannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>arrogant, presumptuous, assuming, assumptive</li>
<li>overweening <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">over-confident</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>self-confident, confident, self-assured, self-sufficient</li>
<li>presuming</li>
<li>reliant</li></ol>
